<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:etter.html>etter</a> (7951)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:etter.html>etter</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ēttar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aitrą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">atter</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Eiter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etter.html>etter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:pus.html>pus</a></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">être</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">creature</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with folk-etymological influence from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etter.html>etter</a></i> (etymology 1).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etter.html>etter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etters.html>etters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ettertje.html>ettertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A nasty person, a <a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>prat</a>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:etterbuil.html>etterbuil</a> (61125)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etter.html>etter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pus.html>pus</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buil.html>buil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hump, bump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etterbuil.html>etterbuil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etterbuil.html>etterbuilen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etterbuil.html>etterbuiltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a localized accumulation of <a href = vnd.unilang:pus.html>pus</a> in the skin; a <span class="Latn" lang="en">boil</span></li></ol>

***eufemisme.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eufemisme.html>eufemisme</a> (32678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Recorded since 1656; from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εὐφημισμός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">euphēmismós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren Latn">euphēmízō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εὔφημος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eúphēmos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">uttering sound of good <a href = vnd.unilang:omen.html>omen</a>, abstaining from inauspicious <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εὖ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eû</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">well</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φήμη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phḗmē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a voice, a prophetic voice, rumor, talk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φάναι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr ***eureka.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eureka.html>eureka</a> (15439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εὕρηκα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">heúrēka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I have found</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> active indicative 1st singular of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εὑρίσκω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">heurískō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I find</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:euthanasie.html>euthanasie</a> (27182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely borrowed. The spelling with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> attested since the 1840s. Before then the Latin-based <i>euthanasia</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> used, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">euthanasia</i> in the seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>Euthanasia <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">medically assisted killing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any gentle or good death.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">evel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ovel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">oevel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">uvil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ubilaz</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> ev (16066)</h1><br></body> 
***eva.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eva.html>eva</a> (4132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eva.html>Eva</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Eve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, referring to the fig leaves the postlapsarian Eve wore to cover her <a href = vnd.unilang:vulva.html>vulva</a> in the Biblical story.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***evacueren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:evacueren.html>evacueren</a> (6949)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">évacuer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:evacueren.html>evacueren</a></strong>
</p>

***even.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> (103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:effen.html>effen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:evan.html>evan</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ebnaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>shortly, briefly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I shall have a look for you <b>shortly</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>for a short period, for a while
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweede.html>tweede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helft.html>helft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> 19e <a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloeide.html>bloeide</a> Vollenhove <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a>.<sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/VollenhoveGeschiedenis">[3]</a></sup></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the second <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of the 19th century, Vollenhove flourished again <b>for a while</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>for a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>; <span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating that the speaker expects that something will require little time or effort.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>Zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Could you please close the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> (<b>for a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a></b>)?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>just as, to the same degree <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">used with an adjective</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:midden.html>midden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloer.html>vloer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stond.html>stond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the middle of the floor there stood a four-metre tall table and a chair <b>just as</b> large beside it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quite, rather

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; '<a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a>' = <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gewicht.html>gewicht</a></span>.

***everzwijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:everzwijn.html>everzwijn</a> (21960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">everswijn</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ever</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zwijn.html>zwijn</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:everzwijn.html>everzwijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:everzwijnen.html>everzwijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:everzwijn.html>everzwijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>boar, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sus.html>Sus</a> scrofa</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">wild boar</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***excelsior.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:excelsior.html>excelsior</a> (38336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:excelsior.html>excelsior</a></i>, comparative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">excelsus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">high</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The name of the stuffing material <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally a trademark.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:excelsior.html>excelsior</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Loftier, yet <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a>, more elevated; ever upward</li>
<li>more surpassing, more excelling</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:excelsior.html>excelsior</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a>  printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The size of type between <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> and brilliant, standardized as 3-point.</li>
<li>Stuffing material (as for furniture and mattresses) made of slender, curled wood shavings, as a substitute for hair.
<ul><li><b>1942</b>, Elliot Paul, <i>The Last Time I Saw Paris</i>, Sickle Moon 2001, p. 91:
<dl><dd>These little mangers, with <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dolls.html>dolls</a> representing Jesus, porcelean <a href = vnd.unilang:josephs.html>Josephs</a> and Marys, wide-eyed cows of papier-mâché, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:excelsior.html>excelsior</a></b> for straw, <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> purchased by pious parents for well-behaved children at Christmas-tide.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">type size</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> minikin</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:excursie.html>excursie</a> (17676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">excursio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a running out, an inroad, invasion, a setting out, beginning of a speech</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">excurrere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>ex</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">currere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***excuus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:excuus.html>excuus</a> (2449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">excuse</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">excuser</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to excuse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">excusare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">release from a charge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ex-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out, away</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">causa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">accusation, legal action</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:excuus.html>excuus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:excuus.html>excusen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:excuses.html>excuses</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:excuus.html>excuusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An excuse, apology, explanation to avoid or alleviate guilt or negative judgement
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verontschuldiging.html>verontschuldiging</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>

***executeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:executeren.html>executeren</a> (9776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:executeren.html>executeren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">executer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:executeren.html>executeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to execute, to kill as punishment</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:executie.html>executie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">execution</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">executio</i>, an <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> noun from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">exequi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to follow out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">out</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sequor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">follow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:executeren.html>executeren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-tie</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:executieve.html>executieve</a> (106992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:executieve.html>executieve</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Inflected form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">executief</i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:executieve.html>executieve</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:executieve.html>executieven</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>often capitalized: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:executieve.html>Executieve</a></b></i>) An executive organ
<ol><li>historically, the name of the three regions' and three linguistic communities' councils of ministers during the early years of federal Belgium (<a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> changed to the equivalent of government)</li></ol>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Vlaamse <b><a href = vnd.unilang:executieve.html>Executieve</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorloper.html>voorloper</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huidige.html>huidige</a> Vlaamse <a href = vnd.unilang:regering.html>Regering</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>The Flemish 'Executive (Council)' <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the precursor of the present Flemish Government</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***exorbitant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a> (83629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">exorbitāns</i>, the present active participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">exorbitō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I go out of the track</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>ex</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orbita</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wheel-track</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">orbit</i>. Compare the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Exceeding proper <a href = vnd.unilang:limits.html>limits</a>; extravagant; excessive or unduly high.
<dl><dd><i>It's a nice car, but they are charging an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a></b> price for it.</i></dd>
<dd><i>You also have to pay <b><a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a></b> interest if you have credit card debt.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b> January 18,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_M._Blow" class="extiw" title="w:Charles M. Blow">Charles M. Blow</a>,  “How expensive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> it to be poor  | print version: <i>International New York Times</i>, 20 January 2015, p. 7 | ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The New York Times">The New York Times</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[M]any low-income people are "unbanked" (not served by a financial institution), and thus nearly eaten alive by <b><a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:fees.html>fees</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:exploderen.html>exploderen</a> (10037)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">exploser</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">explode</i>. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">explosion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">explōsiōnis</i>, genitive form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">explōsio</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">explōdo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I drive out by clapping</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ex-</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">plōdo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I clap or strike</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For more information see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">explode</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
